<script nonce="">
  'use strict'

  !(function () {
    const mainContainer = document.querySelector('.special-led_3-pop-up-creative');
    const firstElem = document.querySelector('.special-led_3-pop-up-first-elem-creative');
    const closeButton = document.querySelector('.special-led_3-pop-up-first-elem-creative__close');
    const videoMain= document.querySelector('.special-led_3-pop-up-fullscreen-video__main');
    const video = document.querySelector('.special-led_3-pop-up-fullscreen-video__main video');
    const playVideoButton = document.querySelector('.special-led_3-pop-up-play');
    const pauseVideoButton = document.querySelector('.special-led_3-pop-up-pause');
    const closePopupButton = document.querySelector('.special-led_3-pop-up-close');
    const muteButton = document.querySelector('.special-led_3-pop-up-mute_btn');
    const videoBtn = document.querySelector('.special-led_3-pop-up-video_btn');
    const modalWrapper = document.querySelector('.special-led_3-pop-up-creative__modal');
    const modal = document.querySelector('.special-led_3-pop-up-creative__modal-blackout');
    const interactiveBox = document.querySelector('.special-led_3-pop-up-interactive__box');
    const closeInteractive = document.querySelector('.special-led_3-pop-up-first-elem-interactive__close_button_icon');

    closeInteractive.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      e.stopPropagation();

      isVideoClosed = true;
      hideVideo();
    });

    const allEvents = document.querySelectorAll('.special-led_3-pop-up-creative__event');
    const eventTarget = document.querySelector('.special-led_3-pop-up-creative__target');
    const eventsArray = [];

    allEvents.forEach((e) => {
      eventsArray.push(e.textContent)
    });

    let isPosterClicked = false;
    let isVideoClosed = false;

    mainContainer.classList.add('special-led_3-pop-up-anim-on');

    video.addEventListener('play', () => {
      playVideoButton.style.display = 'none';
      pauseVideoButton.style.display = '';
    });

    video.addEventListener('pause', () => {
      playVideoButton.style.display = '';
      pauseVideoButton.style.display = 'none';
    });

    video.addEventListener('ended', () => {
      hideVideo();
    });

    playVideoButton.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      e.stopPropagation();
      video.play();
    });

    pauseVideoButton.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      e.stopPropagation();
      video.pause();
    });

    function sendAction(eventNumber) {
      window.open(eventsArray[eventNumber], eventTarget.textContent);
    }

    function showHeart() {
      isPosterClicked = true;
      firstElem.classList.add('clicked');

      const params = {
        container: interactiveBox,
        renderer: 'svg',
        loop: 0,
        autoplay: false,
        path: 'https://banners.adfox.ru/240213/adfox/2881155/5e4b2d72d2dffc4ca02887d329419c14_data.json',
      };

      let anim;

      requestAnimationFrame(() => {
        firstElem.style.visibility = 'hidden';
        modalWrapper.removeAttribute('style');
        interactiveBox.removeAttribute('style');
      });

      modal.style.opacity = '1';
      anim = bodymovin.loadAnimation(params);

      anim.addEventListener("complete", function() {
        if (!isVideoClosed) {
          showVideo();
        }
      });

      setTimeout(()=> {
        anim.play();
      }, 200);
    }

    function showVideo() {
      const videoContainer = document.querySelector('.special-led_3-pop-up-fullscreen-video__container');

      requestAnimationFrame(() => {
        videoContainer.removeAttribute('style');

        setTimeout(()=> {
          videoMain.style.transform = 'scale(1)';
          video.play();
        }, 0);
      });

      const closeButtonContainer = document.querySelector('.special-led_3-pop-up-first-elem-interactive__close_button');
      closeButtonContainer.classList.add('hidden');        
    }

    function hideVideo() {
      video.pause();

      requestAnimationFrame(() => {
        firstElem.style.visibility = '';
        modalWrapper.style.display = 'none';
        modal.style.opacity = '0';
      });
    }

    muteButton.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      e.stopPropagation();

      if (video.muted) {
        muteButton.classList.remove('muted');
        video.muted = false;
      } else {
        muteButton.classList.add('muted');
        video.muted = true;
      }
    });

    closePopupButton.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      e.stopPropagation();
      new Image().src = eventsArray[4];
      hideVideo();
    });

    videoBtn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      e.stopPropagation();
      sendAction(3);
    });

    firstElem.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      e.stopPropagation();
      video.src = 'https://banners.adfox.ru/240212/adfox/2881155/14e8695c2e65ffc66097e6d254330e81_LED3_TVPST_30_Love_4_Uzhe_HD_1.mp4';
      video.play();
      video.pause();

      if (isPosterClicked) {
        sendAction(5);
      } else {
        new Image().src = eventsArray[0];
        showHeart();
      }
    });

    closeButton.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      e.stopPropagation();
      new Image().src = eventsArray[2];
      mainContainer.remove();
    });
  })()
